  ;(function() {
    let previousBreakpoint = null;
    let appBarMutationObAdded;
    const floatingChainWrapper = document.querySelector(".floating-chain-wrapper-1095");
    const closeTrayEl = document.querySelector('div[data-role="close-tray"]');

    function initFloatingChain() {
      const viewportWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;

      // Only set "floating" functionality on desktop
      if (viewportWidth >= 800 && checkBreakpointChange('desktop')) {
        setFloatingChainStyles(true);
      } else if (viewportWidth < 800 && checkBreakpointChange('mobile')) {
        setFloatingChainStyles(false);
      }
    }
    
    function handleAppBarMutations() {
      appBarMutationObAdded = true
      const appBar = document.getElementById('app-bar-sticky');
      if (appBar) {
        let appBarHeight;
        let observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
          mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
            let currentAppBarHeight = appBar.clientHeight
            if (currentAppBarHeight !== appBarHeight) {
              floatingChainWrapper.style.top = currentAppBarHeight + 0 + 'px'
              appBarHeight = currentAppBarHeight
            }
          });
        });
        observer.observe(appBar, { attributes: true, childList: true });
      }
    }

    function checkBreakpointChange(currentBreakpoint) {
      const isBreakpointChanged = !previousBreakpoint || previousBreakpoint !== currentBreakpoint;
      previousBreakpoint = currentBreakpoint;
      return isBreakpointChanged;
    }

    function setFloatingChainStyles(setToSticky) {
      const classListAction = setToSticky ? 'add' : 'remove';
      if (closeTrayEl) {
          closeTrayEl.classList[classListAction]('overflow-x-inherit');
      }
      floatingChainWrapper.classList[classListAction]('sticky');
      floatingChainWrapper.classList[classListAction]('z-index-29');

      // Add mutation observer to check if the height of appbar changes
      setToSticky ? !appBarMutationObAdded && handleAppBarMutations() : floatingChainWrapper.style.top = '0'
    }

    initFloatingChain();
    window.addEventListener('resize', initFloatingChain);
  })();
</script> <div class="pb-container"> </div> </aside> </div> </article> <section id="bottom" class="full-columns container"> <div class="wrapper clearfix pb-curated full pb-feature pb-layout-item pb-f-ads-dfp" data-pb-name="DFP Ad" data-pb-curated="curated" data-pb-id="article-mobile-bottom-leaderboard" id="fnFwI526zkWRcs"> <div class="pb-ad pb-ad-prod ad-320x50 hddn-dktp relative&#32;trb_ad_st_m stuck hddn-dktp"> <div class="ad-caption-text align-center uppercase">Advertisement</div> <div class="trb_st_cl " tabindex="0" aria-label="Close Ad" role="button" aria-pressed="false"> <svg class="closeSticky" focusable="false"> <use xlink:href="#close-sticky"/> </svg> </div> <div id="sports_preps_football_1664" class="hddn" data-optimera-measure="trb_ad_728x90/320x50_2_/sports/highschool/football/os-sp-ocp-tohopekaliga-1016-20201017-7ayzjabyifdb" data-ad-mobile-sticky> </div> </div> <script>

window.pageBuilder._getJson = window.pageBuilder._getJson || function(url, success, failure) {
    var xmlhttp;
    failure = failure|| function () {};
    if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
        xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
    } else {
        xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
    }
    xmlhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (xmlhttp.readyState == 4) {
            if(xmlhttp.status == 200){
                try {
                    success.call(null, JSON.parse(xmlhttp.responseText));
                } catch (e) {
                    failure.call(null, xmlhttp, e)
                }
            } else  {
                failure.call(null, xmlhttp);
            }
        }
    };
    xmlhttp.open("GET", url, true);
    xmlhttp.send();

window.pageBuilder.loadAsyncFeatures = window.pageBuilder.loadAsyncFeatures || function () {
        var d = window.document;
        var scriptsToAdd = [];
        var featuresLoaded = [];
        function injectAsyncFeatures(apiResp){
            for(var fid in apiResp){
                if (!apiResp.hasOwnProperty(fid)) continue;

                var element = d.getElementById(fid);
                var resources = apiResp[fid].pageResources || {};
                element.outerHTML = apiResp[fid].rendering;
                element = d.getElementById(fid); //update the element
                var scripts = Array.prototype.slice.call(element.getElementsByTagName("script"));
                for (var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++) {
                    if (scripts[i].src != "") {
                        var s = d.createElement("script");
                        s.setAttribute("src", scripts[i].src);
                        d.body.appendChild(s);
                    }
                    else {
                        window.pageBuilder._executeAsyncFeatureScripts(scripts[i].innerHTML); //eval isn't evil always.
                    }
                }
                for(var file in resources) {
                    if(resources.hasOwnProperty(file) && file.endsWith(".js")) {
                        resources[file].forEach(function(src){
                            if (scriptsToAdd.indexOf(src) === -1) { scriptsToAdd.push(src) }
                        });
                    }
                }
                featuresLoaded.push(element);
            }
            scriptsToAdd.forEach(function (src) {
                var s = d.createElement("script");
                s.setAttribute("src", src);
                d.body.appendChild(s);
            });
            featuresLoaded.forEach(function(element){
                window.pageBuilder.featureLoaded(element);
            });
        }
    var url = _context + "/api/v2/async/features?rid="+_rid+"&contentUri="+_uri;
    window.pageBuilder._getJson(url, function(resp) { injectAsyncFeatures(resp)});
};
